< Review>
Convenient drug store with limited groceries. Totally love that I can do drive thru though I haven't tried since reduction in hours. I usually avoid the peak evening times and there is usually less than 2 cars in front.  Sometimes you need to push the button several times. Waiting inside can mean lots of standing in line.  Recently the store stopped operating 24/7 so with shorter hours (currently 9 AM to 9 PM), it's less convenient.  There are the occasional panhandlers at the front entrance. They've added Electrical charging parking which reduces close in parking spots.<//Review>

< text>
I rarely like to go here for a few reasons. First, there are pretty much always homeless people hanging around. It's uncomfortable for a mother alone with her baby in a stroller.

It is the only pharmacy within walking distance and the closet pharmacy by a good amount. I went in one time to buy some detergent and the prices were so outlandish I went all the way home and drove to target! Also, the pharmacy is not only super popular but very inefficient.

This may be with any pharmacy but our experience was pretty lousy. My doctor called in a med and when I went to go pick it up they said it would be processing for maybe the entire day! They told me they would call me when it was ready but they never called! I finally had to call myself late in the day and they said to just come at the end of the day (5 pm) and it should be ready. So I waited in a super long line and finally made it to the counter to pick up my med.

The woman at the register was not a pharmacist. She was actually pretty slow and seemed like she had no idea what she was doing. She asked for my insurance card and I told her no I only have kaiser and the card won't help. She argued with me and told me to give her the card so she could check. I thought it would take a minute but it took forever! And in the end, of course, it didn't work.

I dream having to come back here to pick up more Rx's but I'm mentally prepared for it to be awful.<//text>

Sunny interior and, if the weather was more favorable, sunny window views as well. This coffeehouse was a warm and encouraging place to work, with a solid wifi and a profusion of power outlets. In the morning (and they do open really early!), the place was quiet, but as the morning progressed, patrons streamed in, including both students and random visitors. <rating>5< /rating>< Review>
Last month I had several occasions to use Sutter Urgent Care. Each time the reception staff were courteous and professional. This has to be a stressful job dealing with people who are in pain, or at the least unhappy they are there to start with.
I was there for a lacerated arm due to a fall. Nurse Shauna D. was the nurse assigned to me. She was very thorough and explained wound care to me. My foot was swollen and she suggested an x-ray. The x-ray determined  a toe was broken.

Dr. Tseng then saw me and showed me the x-ray and explained my options.He was very nice and very courteous.

The second time, I again saw nurse Shauna D. For an infection. She went above and beyond to make sure I had lab tests and was prescribed the proper antibiotics and to arrange an appointment with my Physician.

After this long posting, it is only necessary to summarize my experience  with Sutter Urgent Care And staff as excellent.< /Review>

The location is very small (6-7 tables), so it might be difficult to get a table if you come with more than few people. As much as it hurts their ambiance, I am also a huge fan of their open kitchen setup. It's always a good feeling knowing that they're not throwing any secret ingredients into my meal behind closed kitchen doors, nommsayin?<//review>

< Name>
Terrence Yacap<//Name>
<date>1613506912022</date><Rating>4<//Rating>< Review>
They just opened so they're very busy and the wait is longer than the norm. The ordering process is relatively fast and straightforward with the available cooked displayed prominently. The workers are very friendly and helpful, trying their best to get the order right and move you along.

I was initially disappointed that they ran out of chocolate chip cookies, but I gave them a break again since they were so new. The wait actually benefited me because they were able to bake up a batch before I received my order.

I assumed that they would just grab the cookies and give them to me immediately, but there was a big backlog so I had to wait for about 15 minutes. I'm sure they're still working out the kinks and trying to determine their production. My only point here is that you'll need to allow for the wait time, so don't stop by if you're in a rush.

Most importantly, the cookies are delicious! In fact, my wife, who does not have a sweet tooth, said it was the best chocolate chip cookie she had ever had. I got a 4-pack so we were able to sample a broad range of what they have to offer. Unfortunately, while I was able to get my chocolate chip, they ran out of the snickerdoodle while I was waiting. I'll have to come back to try that and get a few more chocolate chips.

I commend them for opening at such a tough time for food service businesses and wish them luck. I'll be back in a few days to buy some gift boxes to hand out to friends as New Year's treats and to grab myself a cookie or two.</Review>
